 Due to work pressure, family stress, financial confusion and other similar problems, people often complain of not sleeping or restless

 But apart from these reasons, there is another reason which affects sleep
 shaayad aapako pataa nahin ho lekin hamaari neend, kaaphi had tak hamaare dinar par bhi nirbhar karti he
 There are some eating and drinking things that make you sleepy, while there are others which can spoil your sleep
 saamaanya taur par ek shaks ko kareeb 7 se 8 ghante kii neend lene kii salaah di jaati he
 In such a situation it is very important to make sure that we do not eat anything at night that causes bad sleep or any other problem
 sone se pehle nahin karen in chizon kaa seven:1
 Caffeine Caffeine has a direct effect on our brain
 caffeine kii maatra vaali kisi bhi cheez ke seven se neend par asar padataa he
 The effect of caffeine persists for up to five hours after taking it
 2
 It is not right to eat very spicy food at a time of very spicy food
 bahut adhik masaaledaar khaanaa khaane se jalan or gas kii samasya ho jaati he
 Which does not cause good sleep
 3
 Meatmeats contain high amounts of fat and protein
 jinhen pachne main kaaphi samay lagata he
 In this case, eating meat during the night can make you restless overnight
 4
 Junk food Junk food contains high amounts of saturated fat
 jise pachne main kaaphi lanbaa samay lagata he
 Eating junk food at night, it is a little difficult to sleep peacefully
 5
 If you are going to eat fruit just before bedtime then stop
 falon main natural sugar hoti he jise pachne main vakt lagata he
